There is really no other way to say this. This mindset is indicative of developmental differences. Environment, parenting, ideals, respect of authority, priority. But it is the worst possible variation of that for the society we all want and need to maintain any structure or hope for the greater collective. The Wild West was in the distant past in this country, and it is glamourized in cinema. It was no picnic. It was a horror in comparison to current day. We exist in a time with perspective to that. And if faced with a reality where everyone basically took the law in to their own hands at any given time, we would surely recognize the horror of it. Just as a society 200 years from now would likely shake their heads at the workings of our own. Being intelligent is partially about not having the hubris of only living in the here and now and learning despite what the west has preached the last few decades, the world is not about YOU. Me culture is a culture on the edge. We do not exist is individual entities in the world we are used to. We have a system, structure, and complex mechanisms in place to sustain us all. Please do not disregard and disrespect that. They all exist only as ideas, that we have impressively conformed to over tens of thousands of years as humans. Order, law, currency, a bartering system, language and communication. Understanding! These are achievements, but are only as relevant as the people continuing their legacy and learning/practicing them. Tiffanys stance here is a step back. One that may be represented more staunchly in downtrodden areas, or communities less fortunate that many others. But that is a long problem to solve. Their is no short solution. Us acting like it is reasonable, acceptable, or relatable in any way gives credence to this poisonous reverse in civility and societal expectation. We must continue to strive to correct the injustices in afflicted areas of the world and our country. And help institute fairer systems. But we cannot alternatively allow the attitude she espoused here to corrupt the greater society. It sounds unfair and it is. But if we are striving for the lesser of two injustices here, choosing civility over understanding in some scenarios must be prioritized.   I wish we could rely on most people to be dually understanding of the world that people like Tiffany Haddish are coming from and live in, and also responsible in decision making for our desired path forward as a whole. But it just so often isn't the case. No one should be cancelled. But if anyone has to be, let us not target the Will Smiths or perpetrators of acts. Let us work towards eradicating viewpoints that will objectively take us BACKWARD, and lead to the loss of those vital skills and achievements I mentioned earlier. We are all striving to get better. It may work for the individual to two steps forward and one step back. On a societal scale, we just aren't that harmonious or light on our feet. A step back in an inevitable decline. Nip it in the bud. Speak harshly to people expressing opinions like Tiffanies. Understand where they are coming from if you wish, but remember the most important thing is to make clear they are advocating for regression for all. Putting themselves ahead of the collective. Totally understandable, but no allowable.
